country_event = {

country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.003
	hidden = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		is_ai = yes
		has_tech = ger_mechanized_artillery_2
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = mechanized_template_ger

		division_template = {
			name = "German Mechanized Division"
			division_names_group = GER_MEC_01
			priority = 1

			regiments = {
				mechanized = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				mechanized = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				mechanized = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				mechanized = { x = 0 y = 3 }

				mechanized = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				mechanized = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				mechanized = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				mechanized = { x = 1 y = 3 }

				motorized_rocket_brigade = { x = 2 y = 0 }
				motorized_rocket_brigade = { x = 2 y = 1 }
				motorized_rocket_brigade = { x = 2 y = 2 }
				motorized_rocket_brigade = { x = 2 y = 3 }

				motorized_anti_tank_brigade = { x = 3 y = 0 }
				motorized_anti_tank_brigade = { x = 3 y = 1 }

				assault_brigade = { x = 4 y = 0 }
			}

			support = {
				armored_engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				motorized_logistics_company = { x = 0 y = 1 }

				mechanized_tank_destroyer = { x = 0 y = 3 }

	}

}

country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.004
	hidden = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		is_ai = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "No Step Back"
			}
			has_tech = ger_medium_tank_chassis_2_2
			has_tech = ger_support_tank_chassis_1_2
			has_tech = ger_assault_tank_2_spg
		}
		else = {
			has_tech = ger_medium_1
			has_tech = ger_support_1
			has_tech = ger_light_1_td
			has_tech = ger_light_1_aa
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = light_armor_template_1_ger
		# add_political_power = 2000

		@ARMOR_DIVISION_MANPOWER = 15000
		@ARMOR_DIVISION_INFANTRY_EQUIPMENT = 542
		@ARMOR_DIVISION_HEAVY_INFANTRY_EQUIPMENT = 250
		@ARMOR_DIVISION_LIGHT_TANK_EQUIPMENT = 15
		@ARMOR_DIVISION_medium_tank_support_chassis = 100
		@ARMOR_DIVISION_MEDIUM_TANK_EQUIPMENT = 125
		@ARMOR_DIVISION_light_tank_destroyer_chassis = 25
		@ARMOR_DIVISION_HEAVY_ARTILLERY_EQUIPMENT = 16
		@ARMOR_DIVISION_SUPPORT_EQUIPMENT = 520
		@ARMOR_DIVISION_MOTORIZED_EQUIPMENT = 248
		@ARMOR_DIVISION_MECHANIZED_EQUIPMENT = 250
		@ARMOR_DIVISION_LIGHT_TANK_ANTI_AIR_EQUIPMENT = 10

		division_template = {
			name = "German Medium Tank Division"
			division_names_group = GER_Arm_01
			template_counter = 127
			priority = 2

			regiments = {
				medium_armor = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				medium_armor = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				medium_armor = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				infantry_support_armor = { x = 0 y = 3 }

				medium_armor = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				medium_armor = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				infantry_support_armor = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				infantry_support_armor = { x = 1 y = 3 }

				assault_brigade = { x = 2 y = 0 }

				mechanized = { x = 3 y = 0 }
				mechanized = { x = 3 y = 1 }
				mechanized = { x = 3 y = 2 }
				mechanized = { x = 3 y = 3 }
				mechanized = { x = 3 y = 4 }

				motorized_heavy_anti_air_brigade = { x = 4 y = 0 }
			}

			support = {
				armored_engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				motorized_logistics_company = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				field_hospital = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				heavy_maintenance_company = { x = 0 y = 3 }
				signal_company = { x = 0 y = 4 }

				armoured_recon = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				heavy_artillery = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				assault = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				light_tank_destroyer = { x = 1 y = 3 }
				#anti_tank = { x = 1 y = 4 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {}
}

country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.005
	hidden = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		is_ai = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "No Step Back"
			}
			date > 1943.1.1
		}
		else = {
			has_tech = ger_medium_3_td
			has_tech = ger_medium_4_spg
			has_tech = ger_medium_4_aa
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = medium_armor_template_2_ger

		division_template = {
			name = "German Adv Medium Tank Division"
			division_names_group = GER_Arm_01

			priority = 2

			regiments = {
				medium_armor = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				medium_armor = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				medium_armor = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				heavy_armor = { x = 0 y = 3 }

				medium_armor = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				medium_armor = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				medium_armor = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				infantry_support_armor = { x = 1 y = 3 }
				infantry_support_armor = { x = 2 y = 4 }

				assault_brigade = { x = 2 y = 0 }

				mechanized = { x = 3 y = 0 }
				mechanized = { x = 3 y = 1 }
				mechanized = { x = 3 y = 2 }
				mechanized = { x = 3 y = 3 }
				mechanized = { x = 3 y = 4 }
			}

			support = {
				armored_engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				motorized_logistics_company = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				field_hospital = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				heavy_maintenance_company = { x = 0 y = 3 }
				signal_company = { x = 0 y = 4 }

				armoured_recon = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				motorized_rocket = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				assault = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				medium_sp_artillery = { x = 1 y = 3 }
				medium_sp_anti_air = { x = 1 y = 4 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {}
}


############## Modern Armor


country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.006
	hidden = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		is_ai = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "No Step Back"
			}
			has_tech = ger_modern_tank_chassis_1
			has_tech = ger_medium_tank_5_spg
		}
		else = {
			has_tech = ger_modern_1
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = medium_armor_template_3_ger

		division_template = {
			name = "German Modern Tank Division"
			division_names_group = GER_Arm_01
			template_counter = 129
			priority = 2

			regiments = {
				modern_armor = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				modern_armor = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				modern_armor = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				modern_armor = { x = 0 y = 3 }

				modern_armor = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				modern_armor = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				modern_armor = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				heavy_armor = { x = 1 y = 3 }

				mechanized = { x = 2 y = 0 }
				mechanized = { x = 2 y = 1 }
				mechanized = { x = 2 y = 2 }
				mechanized = { x = 2 y = 3 }

				medium_sp_artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 0 }
				medium_sp_artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 1 }
				medium_sp_artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 2 }

			}

			support = {
				armored_engineer_modern = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				motorized_logistics_company = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				field_hospital = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				heavy_maintenance_company = { x = 0 y = 3 }
				signal_company = { x = 0 y = 4 }

				armoured_recon = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				medium_tank_destroyer = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				assault = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				medium_sp_artillery = { x = 1 y = 3 }
				medium_sp_anti_air = { x = 1 y = 4 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {}
}

				modern_armor = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				modern_armor = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				modern_armor = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				heavy_armor = { x = 1 y = 3 }

				modern_sp_artillery_brigade = { x = 2 y = 0 }
				modern_sp_artillery_brigade = { x = 2 y = 1 }
				modern_tank_destroyer_brigade = { x = 2 y = 2 }

				mechanized = { x = 3 y = 0 }
				mechanized = { x = 3 y = 1 }
				mechanized = { x = 3 y = 2 }
				mechanized = { x = 3 y = 3 }

			}

			support = {
				armored_engineer_modern = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				motorized_logistics_company = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				field_hospital = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				heavy_maintenance_company_modern = { x = 0 y = 3 }
				signal_company = { x = 0 y = 4 }

				armoured_recon = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				modern_tank_destroyer = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				modern_sp_artillery = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				modern_sp_anti_air = { x = 1 y = 3 }
				assault = { x = 1 y = 4 }
			}
		}

		set_technology = {
			modern_oil_processing = 1
			superior_oil_processing = 1
			superior_rubber_processing = 1
		}
	}

	option = {}

############## Heavy Armor

country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.008
	hidden = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		is_ai = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "No Step Back"
			}
			has_tech = ger_medium_tank_5_spg
			has_tech = ger_heavy_tank_chassis_3
			OR = {
				has_tech = ger_heavy_tank_2_td
				has_tech = ger_heavy_tank_1_td
			}
		}
		else = {
			has_tech = ger_medium_4_spg
			has_tech = ger_medium_4_aa
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = heavy_armor_template_1_ger
		division_template = {
			name = "German Heavy Tank Division"
			division_names_group = GER_Arm_01
			template_counter = 131
			priority = 2

			regiments = {
				heavy_armor = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				heavy_armor = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				heavy_armor = { x = 0 y = 2 }

				heavy_armor = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				heavy_armor = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				heavy_armor = { x = 1 y = 2 }

				heavy_armor = { x = 2 y = 0 }
				heavy_armor = { x = 2 y = 1 }
				heavy_armor = { x = 2 y = 2 }

				heavy_tank_destroyer_brigade = { x = 3 y = 0 }

				mechanized = { x = 4 y = 0 }
				mechanized = { x = 4 y = 1 }
				mechanized = { x = 4 y = 2 }
				mechanized = { x = 4 y = 3 }
				mechanized = { x = 4 y = 4 }
			}

			support = {
				armored_engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				motorized_logistics_company = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				field_hospital = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				heavy_maintenance_company = { x = 0 y = 3 }
				signal_company = { x = 0 y = 4 }

				armoured_recon = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				heavy_tank_destroyer = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				assault = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				medium_sp_artillery = { x = 1 y = 3 }
				medium_sp_anti_air = { x = 1 y = 4 }
			}
		}

	}

	option = {}
}

country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.011
	hidden = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = RCZ
		is_ai = yes
		GER = {
			is_ai = yes
			has_capitulated = yes
			has_country_flag = RCZ_garrison_flag
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Festungs-Division" }
	}
	option = {}
}




################################################# Germany is the one conquering




#Poland
country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.101
	hidden = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		89 = {
			CONTROLLER = {
				NOT = {
					tag = RPO
					tag = GER
				}
				OR = {
					is_subject_of = GER
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = RPO
			}
			RPO = { set_state_controller = 89 }
		}
		else = {
			GER = { set_state_controller = 89 }
		}
	}

	option = {}

}

################################################# Oppose Hitler




country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.201
	title = ger_armor.201.t
	desc = ger_armor.201.d

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		has_completed_focus = GER_prepare_the_opposition
		NOT = { has_global_flag = GER_civil_war }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = GER_civil_war_end }
		date > 1938.1.1
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			activate_mission = GER_hitler_anschluss
			if = {
				limit = {
					AUS = { is_guaranteed_by = ITA }
				}

				ITA = {
					country_event = { id = ita_armor.828 days = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ger_armor.201.a
	}

	option = {
		name = ger_armor.201.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = ger_civil_war_anschluss
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.209
	title = ger_armor.209.t
	desc = ger_armor.209.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_coup_failed

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = GER_civil_war_end
			unlock_national_focus = GER_rhineland
			unlock_national_focus = GER_anti_comitern_pact
			unlock_national_focus = GER_west_wall_border_watch
			unlock_national_focus = GER_four_year_plan
			unlock_national_focus = GER_appoint_hermann_goring
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_the_opposition_dynamic_modifier }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_german_industry_dynamic_modifier }
			remove_ideas = GER_shadow_cabinet
			remove_ideas = GER_secret_training_camps
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = GER_continue_with_schacht }
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = GER_continue_with_schacht
					uncomplete_children = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = GER_prepare_the_opposition }
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = GER_prepare_the_opposition
					uncomplete_children = yes
				}
			}
			every_character = {
				limit = {
					has_trait = trait_GER_wehrmacht
				}
				set_character_flag = GER_character_purged_flag
				GER = { retire_character = PREV }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ger_armor.209.a
	}
}

						division = "division_template = \"German Infantry Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
						owner = GNS
						count = GNS.ger_civil_war_infantry_divisions_counter_var
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Light Panzer Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
						owner = GNS
						count = GNS.ger_civil_war_armor_divisions_counter_var
					}
				}
				set_popularities = {
					fascism = 100
				}
				promote_character = GER_adolf_hitler
				add_ideas = economy_fatigue_38
				set_variable = { economic_fatigue = 38 }
				add_ideas = limited_exports
				add_ideas = extensive_conscription
				add_ideas = partial_economic_mobilisation
				add_ideas = national_socialism
				add_ideas = GER_bitter_loser
				add_ideas = GER_okh
				add_ideas = relaxed_industry
				add_ideas = GER_autarky_idea
				add_ideas = GER_ineffective_air_minstry
				add_ideas = internal_conflict
			}
			capital_scope = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"German Infantry Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
					owner = GER
					count = GER.opp_civil_war_infantry_divisions_counter_var
					prioritize_location = 9517
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"German Panzer Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
					owner = GER
					count = GER.opp_civil_war_armor_divisions_counter_var
					prioritize_location = 9517
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = GER_reach_out_to_communist_remnants
				}
				division_template = {
					name = "Kommunistische Abteilung"
					is_locked = yes

					division_names_group = GER_Inf_01

					regiments = {
						heavy_militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }

						militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }

						heavy_militia = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						militia = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						militia = { x = 1 y = 2 }

						heavy_militia = { x = 2 y = 0 }
						militia = { x = 2 y = 1 }
						militia = { x = 2 y = 2 }
					}
					support = {
						engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						horse_field_hospital = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						horse_logistics_company = { x = 0 y = 2 }

						recon = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						artillery = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					}
				}
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Kommunistische Abteilung\" start_experience_factor = 0.7 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
						owner = GER
						count = 6
						prioritize_location = 9517
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = GER_call_upon_the_freikorps
				}
				division_template = {
					name = "Freikorp Infanterie Division"
					template_counter = 123
					priority = 1

					regiments = {
						heavy_infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						heavy_infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						heavy_infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }

						heavy_infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						heavy_infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						heavy_infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }

						heavy_infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
						heavy_infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
						heavy_infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }

						artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 0 }
						artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 1 }
						artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 2 }
					}

					support = {
						engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						motorized_logistics_company = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						heavy_artillery = { x = 0 y = 2 }

						recon = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						field_hospital = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					}
				}
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Freikorp Infanterie Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.7 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
						owner = GER
						count = 12
						prioritize_location = 9517
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = GER_find_former_weimar_officials
				}
				activate_advisor = GER_heinrich_bruning
				activate_advisor = GER_wilhelm_groener
				activate_advisor = GER_kurt_schumacher
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = train_equipment_1 amount = 800 producer = GER }
			}
			add_stability = 0.5
			news_event = { id = wtt_news.1 hours = 6 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ger_armor.210.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GER_civil_war_hungary_flag
				NOT = { has_war_with = HUN }
				HUN = { is_subject = no }
				OR = {
					HUN = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
					HUN = {
						is_in_faction = no
					}
				}
			}
			give_military_access = HUN
			HUN = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = GNS
					type = topple_government
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GER_civil_war_hungary_flag
				NOT = { has_war_with = AUS }
				AUS = { is_subject = no }
				OR = {
					AUS = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
					AUS = {
						is_in_faction = no
					}
				}
			}
			give_military_access = AUS
			AUS = {
				give_military_access = HUN
			}
			AUS = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = GNS
					type = topple_government
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.211
	title = ger_armor.211.t
	desc = ger_armor.211.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_speech

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #disagree
		name = ger_armor.211.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				strength_ratio = { tag = GER ratio < 0.5 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				has_opinion = { target = GER value > 99 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				strength_ratio = { tag = GER ratio < 0.3 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				strength_ratio = { tag = GER ratio < 0.2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				strength_ratio = { tag = GER ratio < 0.1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = GER
				is_subject = no
			}
			remove_from_faction = POL #kicked from faction
		}

		effect_tooltip = {
			GER = {
				add_state_claim = 85
				add_state_claim = 798
				add_state_claim = 797
				add_state_claim = 86
				add_state_claim = 762
				create_wargoal = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = POL
					generator = { 85 798 797 86 762 }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = {
				country_event = { id = ger_armor.212 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #agree
		name = ger_armor.211.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FRA = { has_completed_focus = FRA_ratify_the_entente }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				any_other_country = {
					is_major = yes
					NOT = { original_tag = FRA }
					has_guaranteed = POL
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				any_other_country = {
					is_major = yes
					is_in_faction_with = POL
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				any_other_country = {
					is_major = no
					has_guaranteed = POL
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				is_in_faction = yes
				NOT = {
					any_other_country = {
						is_major = yes
						is_in_faction_with = POL
					}
				}
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			GER = {
				transfer_state = 85
				transfer_state = 798
				transfer_state = 797
				transfer_state = 86
				transfer_state = 762
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = POL
					relation = guarantee
					active = yes
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = {
				country_event = {
					id = ger_armor.213 days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### Warsaw Conference

# Britain
country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.214
	title = ger_armor.214.t
	desc = {
		text = ger_armor.214.d
		trigger = { NOT = { has_war_with = GER } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ger_armor.214.d_2
		trigger = { has_war_with = GER }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ger_armor.214.d_3
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_war_with = GER }
			tag = HOL
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_politician_speech

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Abandon the Poles
		name = ger_armor.214.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.3
				has_government = communism
				POL = { has_government = communism }
			}
			modifier = {
				has_global_flag = GER_has_started_war
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_war_with = GER }
			is_puppet = no # can't do anything if puppet
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = ENG_no_further_appeasement
			}
			add_political_power = -200
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = HOL
			}
			ENG = { country_event = ger_armor.214 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = ENG
			}
			FRA = { country_event = ger_armor.215 }
		}
		POL = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = western_betrayal }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = HOL
				POL = { is_guaranteed_by = HOL }
			}
			HOL = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
   					country = POL
   					relation = guarantee
   					active = no
  				}
  				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = ignore
					id = "POL"
					value = 100
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = ENG
				POL = { is_guaranteed_by = ENG }
			}
			ENG = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
   					country = POL
   					relation = guarantee
   					active = no
  				}
  				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = ignore
					id = "POL"
					value = 100
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				POL = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			remove_from_faction = POL
		}
	}
	option = { # Support the Poles
		name = ger_armor.214.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					tag = ENG
				}
				has_completed_focus = ENG_no_further_appeasement
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				has_government = communism
				POL = { has_government = communism }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = POL
						has_war_with = GER
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						GER = {
							has_country_flag = GER_return_austria_flag
						}
						NOT = { has_global_flag = GER_has_started_war }
					}
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = GER
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			remove_from_faction = GER
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = GER
				is_faction_leader = no
			}
			GER = { remove_from_faction = ENG }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = ENG_no_further_appeasement }
			}
			add_political_power = -200
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = condemn_aggression }
		effect_tooltip = {
			GER = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = POL
					generator = { 85 798 797 86 762 188 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				POL = { is_in_faction = no }
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT #this may in fact be ROOT, since countries are in a faction with themselves!
				}
				add_to_faction = POL
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = HOL
			}
			POL = {
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "HOL"
					value = 200
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = HOL
			}
			POL = {
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "ENG"
					value = 200
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = HOL }
				FRA = {
					NOT = { has_war_with = POL }
				}
			}
			FRA = { country_event = ger_armor.216 }
		}
		POL = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = offered_support }
		}
	}
}

# France (Britain Backs Down)
country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.215
	title = ger_armor.214.t
	desc = ger_armor.215.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chamberlain_announce

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Follow Britain's lead
		name = ger_armor.215.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = FRA_the_pcf_direction }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.3
				has_government = communism
				POL = { has_government = communism }
			}
			modifier = {
				has_global_flag = GER_has_started_war
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		POL = {
			country_event = ger_armor.220
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = western_betrayal }
		}
		add_war_support = 0.1
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = POL
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_other_country = { #check if POL and FRA are the only countries in this faction
							NOT = { original_tag = POL }
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				dismantle_faction = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = POL
				is_faction_leader = no
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				remove_from_faction = FRA
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				POL = { is_guaranteed_by = FRA }
			}
			FRA = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
   					country = POL
   					relation = guarantee
   					active = no
  				}
  				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = ignore
					id = "POL"
					value = 100
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Support the POLchs alone
		name = ger_armor.215.b
		trigger = { is_puppet = no }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AND = {
						GER = {
							has_country_flag = GER_return_austria_flag
						}
						NOT = { has_global_flag = GER_has_started_war }
					}
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 6
				has_government = communism
				POL = { has_government = communism }
			}
		}
		add_war_support = 0.05
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = POL
				has_completed_focus = FRA_ratify_the_entente
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = FRA_the_pcf_direction }
			}
			add_political_power = -100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = FRA_ratify_the_entente }
					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = POL }
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = FRA_the_pcf_direction }
				}
			}
			add_political_power = -200
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = condemn_aggression }
		POL = {
			country_event = ger_armor.219
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = offered_support }
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = ger_armor.222
			effect_tooltip = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = POL
					generator = { 85 798 797 86 762 188 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
			ENG = {
				country_event = ger_armor.217
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
					remove_from_faction = FRA
					else = {
						FRA = { remove_from_faction = ENG }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
			if = {
				limit = { GER = { is_faction_leader = yes } }
				GER = {
					remove_from_faction = FRA
				}
				else = {
					remove_from_faction = GER
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				is_faction_leader = yes
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = POL }
				POL = { is_in_faction = no }
			}
			add_to_faction = POL
			POL = {
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "FRA"
					value = 200
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction = no
					AND = {
						is_faction_leader = no
						is_in_faction_with = ENG
					}
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
				POL = { is_in_faction = no }
			}
			create_faction = "french_alliance"
			set_rule = { can_create_factions = yes }
			add_to_faction = POL
			POL = {
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "FRA"
					value = 200
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = no
				POL = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			POL = { add_to_faction = FRA }
			FRA = {
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "POL"
					value = 200
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = FRA_ratify_the_entente } }
			add_stability = 0.05
		}
	}
}

# France (Britain Supports the Polish)

	desc = ger_armor.216.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_POLch_soldiers_01

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Support
	option = {
		name = ger_armor.216.a
		trigger = {
			is_subject = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = POL }
				NOT = { has_guaranteed = POL }
			}
			give_guarantee = POL
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = no
			}
			ENG = { add_to_faction = FRA }
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = "ENG"
				value = 200
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = POL
				has_completed_focus = FRA_ratify_the_entente
				is_faction_leader = yes
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
			}
			add_to_faction = ENG #Britain joins the little entente
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { is_subject_of = ENG }
				ROOT = { add_to_faction = PREV }
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = condemn_aggression }
		POL = {
			country_event = ger_armor.218
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = offered_support }
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = ger_armor.221
			effect_tooltip = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = POL
					generator = { 85 798 797 86 762 188 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#Abandon
	option = {
		name = ger_armor.216.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = POL }
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = FRA_the_pcf_direction }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				has_global_flag = GER_has_started_war
				OR = {
					POL = { exists = no }
					POL = { is_puppet_of = GER }
					DEN = { exists = no }
					DEN = { is_puppet_of = GER }
					HOL = { exists = no }
					HOL = { is_puppet_of = GER }
					BEL = { exists = no }
					BEL = { is_puppet_of = GER }
					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER } #FRA doesn't care if in faction
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				POL = { is_guaranteed_by = FRA }
			}
			FRA = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
   					country = POL
   					relation = guarantee
   					active = no
  				}
  				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = ignore
					id = "POL"
					value = 100
				}
			}
		}
		POL = {
			country_event = ger_armor.218
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = western_betrayal }
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = ger_armor.221
			effect_tooltip = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = POL
					generator = { 85 798 797 86 762 188 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Poland (Abandoned)
country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.220
	title = ger_armor.220.t
	desc = ger_armor.220.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_czech_soldiers_01

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Surrender East Prussia
		name = ger_armor.220.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = { # Decrease chance POL resists if AUS isn't taken
				AUS = { exists = yes }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = { # If they stand a chance they will fight
				factor = 0
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = GER
					ratio > 0.75
				}
				NOT = {
					any_neighbor_country = {
						NOT = { tag = GER }
						is_in_faction_with = GER
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #if you lead a faction, fight
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5 #if you are in a faction, maybe fight
				is_faction_leader = no
				is_in_faction = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.05 #if you are in a faction with a major, probably fight
				is_faction_leader = no
				is_in_faction = yes
				any_allied_country = {
					is_major = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_puppet = yes
				NOT = { is_puppet_of = GER } #puppeted POL wouldn't surrender Sudetenland otherwise
			}
			modifier = { # Increase it again if other bordering nations are in Axis
				any_neighbor_country = {
					NOT = { tag = GER }
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
				factor = 2.0
			}
		}
		GER = { country_event = ger_armor.224 }
	}
	option = { # Refuse anyway
		name = ger_armor.220.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = GER
					ratio < 0.5
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = GER
					ratio < 0.3
				}
			}
		}
		GER = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = GER_demand_sudetenland_rejected }
			set_global_flag = POL_refused_sudetenland
			country_event = ger_armor.223
			effect_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						POL = {
							is_in_faction_with = GER
						}
					}
					GER = { remove_from_faction = POL }
				}
				create_wargoal = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = POL
					generator = { 85 798 797 86 762 188 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Ask hungary to become monarchist
country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.225
	title = ger_armor.225.t
	desc = ger_armor.225.d

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #accept
		name = ger_armor.225.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 7
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				has_opinion = {
					target = GER
					value > 50
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					not = {
						has_completed_focus = HUN_elect_a_king
					}
				}
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = HUN_faith_in_the_regency
					uncomplete_children = yes
					refund_political_power = no
				}
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = HUN_legacy_of_gombos
					uncomplete_children = yes
					refund_political_power = no
				}
				complete_national_focus = HUN_elect_a_king
			}

			GER = {
				add_to_faction = root
				country_event = ger_armor.227
			}
		}

	}
	option = { #refuse
		name = ger_armor.225.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 3
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_completed_focus = HUN_elect_a_king
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = Start_civil_war_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					not = {
						has_completed_focus = HUN_elect_a_king
					}
				}
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = HUN_faith_in_the_regency
					uncomplete_children = yes
					refund_political_power = no
				}
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = HUN_legacy_of_gombos
					uncomplete_children = yes
					refund_political_power = no
				}
				complete_national_focus = HUN_elect_a_king
			}
			GER = {
				add_to_faction = ROOT
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = democratic
				states = { 891 890 154 }
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = HUN
					has_war_with = root
				}
				GER = {
					add_to_war = {
						targeted_alliance = HUN
						enemy = prev
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

# give back austria
country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.227
	title = ger_armor.227.t
	desc = ger_armor.227.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ger_armor.227.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = GER_AI_RANDOM_KAISER_BRITAIN
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_ai_behavior
						option = KAISER_BRITAIN
					}
					has_country_flag = GER_AI_RANDOM_PRUSSIA
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_ai_behavior
						option = PRUSSIA
					}
				}
			}
		}
		AUS = {
			every_core_state = {
				remove_core_of = GER
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = root
				is_core_of = AUS
			}
			transfer_state_to = HUN
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ger_armor.227.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = GER_AI_RANDOM_KAISER
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_ai_behavior
						option = KAISER
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.301
	hidden = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_leader = { character = GER_adolf_hitler ruling_only = yes }
		tag = GER
		date > 1944.1.1
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_leader_portrait = {
			portrait = GFX_adolf_hitler_1944
		}
	}

	option = {}

}

country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.604
	hidden = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		is_ai = yes
		is_historical_focus_on = yes
		country_exists = YUG
		NOT = { is_in_faction_with = YUG }
		NOT = { has_war_with = YUG }
		OR = {
			has_war_with = GRE
			is_in_faction_with = GRE
		}
		date > 1941.4.6
		has_government = fascism
		has_war = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		declare_war_on = {
			target = YUG
			type = take_state_focus
			generator = { 102 }
		}
	}

	option = {}

}

country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.701
	title = ger_armor.701.t
	desc = {
		text = ger_armor.701.d
		trigger = {
			tag = CHI
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ger_armor.701.e
		trigger = {
			tag = JAP
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ger_armor.701.a
		trigger = {
			tag = CHI
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 3
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			GER = {
				send_equipment = {
					target = CHI
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = 25000
					old_prioritised = yes
				}
			}
			GER = {
				send_equipment = {
					target = CHI
					type = artillery_equipment
					amount = 500
					old_prioritised = yes
				}
			}
			GER = {
				send_equipment = {
					target = CHI
					type = light_tank_chassis
					amount = 250
					old_prioritised = yes
				}
			}
			GER = { transfer_state = 743 }
			CHI = {
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = ger_extra_chi_diplomacy_focus }
			}
			JAP = {
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = extra_supported_the_chinese }
			}
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = ger_armor.702
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ger_armor.701.a
		trigger = {
			tag = JAP
		}

		}

				}
			}
			GER = { transfer_state = 743 }
		}

################################################# Fate of YUG Germany





country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.711
	title = ger_armor.711.t
	desc = ger_armor.711.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ger_armor.711.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = ITA
				is_in_faction_with = HUN
				is_in_faction_with = BUL
			}
		}
		economy_fatigue_level_down_4 = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				CRO = { exists = no }
			}
			release = CRO
		}
		CRO = {
			transfer_state = 109
			transfer_state = 999
			transfer_state = 103
			transfer_state = 104
			transfer_state = 913
			transfer_state = 907
			hidden_effect = {
				load_focus_tree = rkcroatia_focus
				inherit_technology = GER
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = ger_inf_1
					amount = 2500
					producer = GER
				}

				add_manpower = 150000
				add_political_power = 350
				add_ideas = partial_economic_mobilisation
			}

			GER = {
				puppet = CRO
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_dlc = "Death or Dishonor" }
					}
					set_autonomy = { target = CRO autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet }
				}
				else = {
					set_autonomy = { target = CRO autonomy_state = autonomy_reichsprotectorate }
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_rk_consumer_goods_expected_value = 0.01 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_dynamic_modifier = {
								modifier = GER_rk_obligations
							}
						}
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = GER_rp_obligations_add_tt
					hidden_effect = {
						add_dynamic_modifier = {
							modifier = GER_rk_obligations
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = GER_rp_obligations_tt
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = ITA
			}
			ITA = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = YUG
					}
					set_state_controller = 102
					set_state_controller = 1022
					set_state_controller = 908
				}
				else = {
					transfer_state = 102
					transfer_state = 1022
					transfer_state = 908
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					add_state_claim = 102
					add_state_claim = 1022
					add_state_claim = 908
				}
				economy_fatigue_level_down_4 = yes
				country_event = { id = ger_armor.837 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = ALB
				}
				ALB = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_war_with = YUG
						}
						set_state_controller = 849
						set_state_controller = 850
						set_state_controller = 105
						hidden_effect = {
							add_state_claim = 849
							add_state_claim = 850
							add_state_claim = 105
						}
					}
					else = {
						transfer_state = 849
						transfer_state = 850
						transfer_state = 105
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				ITA = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_war_with = YUG
						}
						set_state_controller = 849
						set_state_controller = 850
						set_state_controller = 105
						hidden_effect = {
							add_state_claim = 849
							add_state_claim = 850
							add_state_claim = 105
						}
					}
					else = {
						transfer_state = 849
						transfer_state = 850
						transfer_state = 105
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = HUN
			}
			HUN = {
				transfer_state = 45
				transfer_state = 888
				hidden_effect = {
					add_state_claim = 45
					add_state_claim = 888
				}
				economy_fatigue_level_down_4 = yes
				country_event = { id = ger_armor.835 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = BUL
			}
			BUL = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = YUG
					}
					set_state_controller = 851
					set_state_controller = 106
				}
				else = {
					transfer_state = 851
					transfer_state = 106
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					add_state_claim = 851
					add_state_claim = 106
				}
				economy_fatigue_level_down_4 = yes
				country_event = { id = ger_armor.836 }
			}
		}
		release = RSE
		RSE = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					GER = { has_war_with = YUG }
				}
				transfer_state = 107
				set_state_controller = 764
				set_state_controller = 108
			}
			else = {
				transfer_state = 107
				transfer_state = 764
				transfer_state = 108
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				add_state_claim = 107
				add_state_claim = 764
				add_state_claim = 108
				set_cosmetic_tag = REN_reichskommissariat
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = fascism
					long_name = RSE_PARTY_NAME_LONG
					name = RSE_PARTY_NAME_SHORT
				}
				GER = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								has_dlc = "Together for Victory"
								has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
							}
						}
						set_autonomy = {
							target = RSE
							autonomy_state = autonomy_reichskommissariat
						}
					}
					else = {
						puppet = RSE
					}
					send_equipment = {
						target = RSE
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 7500
						old_prioritised = yes
					}
					send_equipment = {
						target = RSE
						type = support_equipment
						amount = 800
						old_prioritised = yes
					}
				}
				add_ideas = GER_reichkommissariats_governments
				add_stability = 0.3
				add_manpower = 25000
				inherit_technology = ROOT
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = ger_inf_0
					amount = 5000
					producer = GER
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = support_equipment_1
					amount = 400
					producer = GER
				}
				load_oob = "REN_Military_Police"
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_by = RSE
				}
				set_garrison_strength = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ger_armor.711.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = ITA

		}

			}

				set_state_controller = 102

				hidden_effect = {

				}
				economy_fatigue_level_down_4 = yes

			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = ALB
				}
				ALB = {
					transfer_state = 849
					transfer_state = 850
					transfer_state = 105
				}
			}
			else = {
				ITA = {
					transfer_state = 849
					transfer_state = 850
					transfer_state = 105
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = HUN
			}
			HUN = {
				transfer_state = 45
				transfer_state = 888
				set_state_controller = 109
				set_state_controller = 907
				hidden_effect = {

					add_state_claim = 907
				}
				economy_fatigue_level_down_4 = yes
				country_event = { id = ger_armor.835 }

		}
		if = {

			}
			BUL = {

					long_name = RSE_PARTY_NAME_LONG

################################################# Croations demand independance





country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.713
	title = ger_armor.713.t
	desc = ger_armor.713.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ustasha

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = GER
		109 = {
			CONTROLLER = {
				OR = {
					tag = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		999 = {
			CONTROLLER = {
				OR = {
					tag = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		103 = {
			CONTROLLER = {
				OR = {
					tag = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { country_exists = YUG }
			YUG = { has_capitulated = yes }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			activate_mission = GER_croats_demand_independance
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ger_armor.713.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			activate_mission = GER_croats_demand_independance
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.798
	title = ger_armor.798.t
	desc = ger_armor.798.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ger_armor.798.a
		GER = { country_event = { id = ger_armor.799 days = 1 } }
		effect_tooltip = {
			GER = {
				create_faction = "Victorian Empires"
				add_to_faction = ENG
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				has_completed_focus = GER_accept_british_naval_dominance
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				has_opinion = {
					target = GER
					value > 85
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				FRA = {
					has_same_ideology = no
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				GER = {
					has_same_ideology = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ger_armor.798.b
		GER = { country_event = { id = ger_armor.800 days = 1 } }
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = ENG
						is_in_faction_with = ENG
						is_subject_of = ENG
					}
				}
				GER = {
					send_embargo = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				has_opinion = {
					target = GER
					value < 86
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				FRA = {
					has_same_ideology = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				GER = {
					has_same_ideology = no
				}
			}
		}
	}

	id = ger_armor.801

		FIN = { remove_country_leader_trait = stout_defender }

country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.805
	title = ger_armor.805.t
	desc = ger_armor.805.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ger_armor.805.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = neutrality_idea
			}
			remove_ideas = neutrality_idea
		}
		851 = { add_claim_by = BUL }
		106 = { add_claim_by = BUL }
		184 = { add_claim_by = BUL }
		731 = { add_claim_by = BUL }
		GER = {
			add_to_faction = BUL
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				GER = { has_war_with = GRE }
				NOT = { has_war_with = GRE }
			}
			add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = GER enemy = GRE hostility_reason = asked_to_join }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				GER = { has_war_with = YUG }
				NOT = { has_war_with = YUG }
			}
			add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = GER enemy = YUG   hostility_reason = asked_to_join }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ger_armor.805.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_completed_focus = BUL_grow_closer_to_germany
			}
		}
		GER = { country_event = { id = ger_armor.806 } }
	}
}

	title = ger_armor.808.t
	desc = ger_armor.808.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ger_armor.807.a
		navy_experience = 40

			name = JAP_german_technological_exchange

			uses = 2
			category = armor
		}
		if = {

				has_dlc = "No Step Back"
				GER = { has_tech = ger_heavy_tank_chassis_3 }
			}
			JAP = {
				set_technology = {
					ger_heavy_tank_chassis_3 = 1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "No Step Back"
				GER = { has_tech = ger_heavy_tank_chassis_2 }
			}
			JAP = {
				set_technology = {
					ger_heavy_tank_chassis_2 = 1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				GER = { has_tech = ger_heavy_3 }
			}
			JAP = {
				set_technology = {
					ger_heavy_3 = 1
				}
			}
		}

			}

				set_technology = {

				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			activate_advisor = gunther_lutjens
		}
		navy_experience = 50
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.820
	title = ger_armor.820.t
	desc = ger_armor.820.d

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		has_war = no
		OR = {
			has_full_control_of_state = 9
			AND = {
				RCZ = {
					is_puppet_of = GER
				}
				RCZ = { has_full_control_of_state = 9 }
			}
			AND = {
				CZE = {
					is_puppet_of = GER
				}
				CZE = { has_full_control_of_state = 9 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ger_armor.820.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "No Step Back"
			}
			set_technology = {
				ger_light_tank_chassis_3 = 1
			}
			add_equipment_production = {
				equipment = {
					type = tank_ger_light_chassis_3
					creator = "GER"
				}
				requested_factories = 5
				progress = 0.4
				efficiency = 100
				industrial_manufacturer = mio:GER_daimler_benz_organization
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_technology = {
				ger_light_3 = 1
			}
			add_equipment_production = {
				equipment = {
					type = ger_light_equipment_3
					creator = "GER"
				}
				requested_factories = 5
				progress = 0.4
				efficiency = 100
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = RCZ
				date > 1939.1.1
				has_dlc = "No Step Back"
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = tank_cze_light_chassis_4 amount = 125 producer = RCZ }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = tank_cze_light_chassis_3 amount = 244 producer = RCZ }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = tank_cze_light_chassis_2 amount = 100 producer = RCZ }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = RCZ
				date > 1938.1.1
				has_dlc = "No Step Back"
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = tank_cze_light_chassis_3 amount = 244 producer = RCZ }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = tank_cze_light_chassis_2 amount = 100 producer = RCZ }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = RCZ
				date > 1937.1.1
				has_dlc = "No Step Back"
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = tank_cze_light_chassis_3 amount = 122 producer = RCZ }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = tank_cze_light_chassis_2 amount = 100 producer = RCZ }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = RCZ
				date > 1939.1.1
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = cze_interwar_equipment_1 amount = 125 producer = RCZ }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = cze_light_equipment_1 amount = 244 producer = RCZ }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = cze_light_equipment_2 amount = 100 producer = RCZ }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = RCZ
				date > 1938.1.1
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = cze_interwar_equipment_1 amount = 244 producer = RCZ }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = cze_light_equipment_1 amount = 100 producer = RCZ }
		}
		else_if = {

################################################# Invade Poland, no focus required





country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.834
	title = ger_armor.834.t
	desc = ger_armor.834.d

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		NOT = { has_war_with = POL }
		NOT = { is_in_faction_with = POL }
		NOT = { POL = { is_subject_of = GER } }
		POL = {
			has_war = yes
			surrender_progress > 0.3
			any_enemy_country = {
				NOT = { original_tag = POL }
			}
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { POL = { is_guaranteed_by = FRA } }
			FRA = { has_capitulated = yes }
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { POL = { is_guaranteed_by = ENG } }
			ENG = { has_capitulated = yes }
			has_global_flag = ENG_fall_of_the_uk
		}
		OR = {
			POL = { is_in_faction = no }
			NOT = {
				POL = {
					any_allied_country = {
						is_major = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ger_armor.834.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				threat > 0.70
			}
		}
#		85 = { add_core_of = GER }
		add_state_claim = 798
		add_state_claim = 797
		add_state_claim = 1000
		add_state_claim = 86
		add_state_claim = 762
		declare_war_on = {
			target = POL
			type = take_state_focus
			generator = { 798 797 86 762 1000 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = DNZ
			}
			annex_country = { target = DNZ transfer_troops = no }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ger_armor.834.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				threat < 0.7
			}
		}
	}
}

				}
			}

		}

			retire = yes
		}
	}

################################################# Why Die for danzig?





country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.857
	title = ger_armor.857.t
	desc = ger_armor.857.d

	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		has_government = fascism
		GER = { has_completed_focus = GER_danzig_or_war }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = GER_planned_offensives }
		has_war_with = POL
		any_enemy_country = {
			is_major = yes
			has_government = democratic
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = GER_lack_of_offensive_plans_initial
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_ideas = GER_lack_of_offensive_plans_initial
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = GER_lack_of_offensive_plans
					days = 120
				}
				set_country_flag = GER_lack_of_offensive_plans_over
			}
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = GER_lack_of_offensive_plans
					days = 120
				}
				set_country_flag = GER_lack_of_offensive_plans_over
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ger_armor.857.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = GER_lack_of_offensive_plans
				days = 120
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = ger_armor.858.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ger_armor.858.a
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = USA
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OWNER = {
						OR = {
							original_tag = ENG
							original_tag = FRA
							original_tag = IRE
							original_tag = HOL
							original_tag = BEL
							original_tag = LUX
							original_tag = DEN

							original_tag = YUG
							original_tag = ALB
							original_tag = BUL
							original_tag = GRE
							original_tag = TUR
							original_tag = LIT
							original_tag = LAT
							original_tag = EST
							original_tag = UKE
							original_tag = UKM
							original_tag = UKN
							original_tag = UKT
							original_tag = UKO
							original_tag = FRT
							original_tag = FRN
							original_tag = FRM
							original_tag = FRS
							original_tag = FRW
							original_tag = FRC
							original_tag = FRP
							original_tag = FRO
							original_tag = FRJ
							original_tag = FRV
							original_tag = FRI
							original_tag = SOV
						}
					}
					CONTROLLER = {
						OR = {
							is_in_faction_with = GER
							is_subject_of = GER
							tag = GER
						}
					}
				}
				CONTROLLER = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = GER
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = THIS
					is_puppet_of = THIS
					tag = THIS
				}
			}
			white_peace = GER
		}
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = afo_news.13 hours = 6 } }
		set_global_flag = ww2_has_ended
		GER = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_army_manpower = {
						size > 3000000
					}
				}
				add_ideas = GER_oversized_wehrmacht
			}
		}
		USA = {
			remove_wargoal = {
				type = all
				target = GER
			}
		}
		USA = {
			remove_wargoal = {
				type = all
				target = ITA
			}
		}
		USA = {
			set_faction_name  = nato_faction
		}
		ITA = {
			remove_wargoal = {
				type = all
				target = SOV
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			remove_wargoal = {
				type = all
				target = ITA
			}
		}
		ENG = {
			remove_wargoal = {
				type = all
				target = GER
			}
		}
		ENG = {
			remove_wargoal = {
				type = all
				target = ITA
			}
		}
		USA = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
				set_rule = { can_not_declare_war = yes }
			}

################################################# War with the USA




country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.860
	title = ger_armor.860.t
	desc = ger_armor.860.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hitler_speech_reichstag

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		has_government = fascism
		has_global_flag = tripartite_pact_signed
		AND = {
			has_war_with = ENG
			ENG = { has_government = democratic }
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				JAP = { has_war_with = USA }
				OR = {
					JAP = { has_government = fascism }
					JAP = { has_government = neutrality }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				ITA = { has_war_with = USA }
				OR = {
					ITA = { has_government = fascism }
					ITA = { has_government = neutrality }
				}
			}
		}
		USA = { has_completed_focus = USA_lend_lease_act }
		USA = { has_government = democratic }
		NOT = { has_war_with = USA }
	}

	option = {
		name = ger_armor.860.a
		declare_war_on = {
			target = USA
			type = annex_everything
		}
		add_political_power = 150
		add_war_support = 0.1
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ger_armor.864 hours = 6 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.875
	title = ger_armor.875.t
	desc = ger_armor.875.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ger_armor.875.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}
		trigger = {
			any_other_country = {
				original_tag = SPR
				has_government = fascism
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				is_subject = no
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Death or Dishonor"
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = SPR
						has_government = fascism
						is_in_faction_with = GER
						is_subject = no
					}
					set_autonomy = {
						target = POR
						autonomy_state = autonomy_reichskommissariat
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = SPR
						has_government = fascism
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						is_subject = no
					}
					puppet = POR
				}
			}
		}
		POR = { country_event = { id = ger_armor.876 hours = 6 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = ger_armor.875.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		POR = { country_event = { id = ger_armor.877 hours = 6 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = ger_armor.875.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = POR
			expire = 0
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.888
	title = ger_armor.888.t
	desc = ger_armor.888.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_coup_failed

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		has_government = fascism
		has_war_with = SOV
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = GER_operation_valkyrie
		}
		OR = {
			has_war_with = FRA
			has_war_with = ENG
			has_war_with = USA
		}
		check_variable = { GER_wehrmacht_attitude = 70 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
		date > 1944.7.13
		OR = {
			202 = { is_controlled_by = SOV }
			206 = { is_controlled_by = SOV }
		}
		OR = {
			surrender_progress > 0.05
			99 = { CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = GER } }
			735 = { CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = GER } }
			22 = { CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = GER } }
			21 = { CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = GER } }
			19 = { CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = GER } }
			23 = { CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = GER } }
			30 = { CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = GER } }
			14 = { CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = GER } }
			15 = { CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = GER } }
			785 = { CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = GER } }
			29 = { CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = GER } }
			6 = { CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = GER } }
			35 = { CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = GER } }
			7 = { CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = GER } }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ger_armor.888.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
		}
		add_war_support = 0.15
		add_stability = -0.1
		retire_character = GER_erwin_rommel
		retire_character = GER_gunther_von_kluge
		retire_character = GER_ludwig_beck
		retire_character = GER_erwin_von_witzleben
		retire_character = GER_erich_hoepner
		custom_effect_tooltip = remove_chief_of_army
		show_ideas_tooltip = GER_ludwig_beck
		custom_effect_tooltip = remove_chief_of_army
		show_ideas_tooltip = franz_halder
		add_to_variable = { GER_wehrmacht_attitude = -50 }
		set_variable = { GER_wehrmacht_influence = 0 }
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = franz_halder
			set_country_flag = valkyrie_purge
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ger_armor.888.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		add_war_support = 0.1
		add_stability = -0.4
		retire_character = GER_ludwig_beck
		retire_character = GER_erwin_von_witzleben
		retire_character = GER_erich_hoepner
		custom_effect_tooltip = remove_chief_of_army
		show_ideas_tooltip = GER_ludwig_beck
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_wehrmacht_attitude = 30 }
		set_variable = { GER_wehrmacht_influence = 0 }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = valkyrie_purge
		}
	}
}

			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_army_size = {
						size < 9

				limit = {
					has_manpower > @ARMOR_DIVISION_MANPOWER
				}
				set_temp_variable = {
					manpower_remove = @ARMOR_DIVISION_MANPOWER
				}
				multiply_temp_variable = {
					manpower_remove = -1

country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.910
	hidden = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		is_ai = yes
		date > 1940.4.24
		date < 1940.7.1
		has_war_with = FRA
		has_army_manpower = { size < 1700000 }
		is_historical_focus_on = yes
	}

	immediate = {

		set_temp_variable = {
			NEEDED_MANPOWER = 170000
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			TOTAL_MANPOWER = ROOT.num_divisions
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			TOTAL_MANPOWER = @AVERAGE_MANPOWER_IN_DIVISION #approximation here
		}
		subtract_from_temp_variable = {
			NEEDED_MANPOWER = TOTAL_MANPOWER
		}
		divide_temp_variable = {
			NEEDED_MANPOWER = @AVERAGE_MANPOWER_IN_DIVISION
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					NEEDED_MANPOWER > 0
				}
			}
			round_temp_variable = NEEDED_MANPOWER
			clamp_temp_variable = { var = NEEDED_MANPOWER max = 35 }
			set_temp_variable = { loop_value = 0 }
			while_loop_effect = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						loop_value < NEEDED_MANPOWER
					}
				}
				810 = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"German Infantry Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.25 start_equipment_factor = 1"
						owner = GER
						count = 1
					}
				}
				IF = {
					limit = {
						has_manpower > @INFANTRY_DIVISION_MANPOWER

country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.911
	hidden = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		is_ai = yes
		date > 1940.6.1
		NOT = { date > 1942.8.1 }
		has_tech = ger_fighter_4
		has_tech = ger_cas_2
		has_tech = ger_tactical_bomber_2
		controls_state = 802
	}

	immediate = {
		add_command_power = 200
		add_political_power = 2000
		set_technology = { ger_anti_air_2 = 1 }
		set_technology = { ger_anti_tank_upgrade_2 = 1 }
		load_oob = "GER_air_3"
	}

	option = {}

}

country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.912
	hidden = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		is_ai = yes
		date > 1941.4.1
		OR = {
			date < 1941.7.1
			has_war_with = SOV
		}
		has_army_manpower = { size < 2800000 }
		is_historical_focus_on = yes
	}

		navy_experience = 300
		delete_unit_template_and_units = {
			division_template = "Light Panzer Division"
			disband = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			NEEDED_MANPOWER = 2500000
		}

		}
		divide_temp_variable = {
			NEEDED_MANPOWER = @AVERAGE_MANPOWER_IN_DIVISION
		}

			limit = {

					NEEDED_MANPOWER > 0
				}

			set_temp_variable = { loop_value = 0 }
			while_loop_effect = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						loop_value < NEEDED_MANPOWER
					}
				}

country_event = {
	id = ger_armor.913
	hidden = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		is_ai = yes
		date > 1941.5.20
		has_army_size = {
			size < 25
			type = armor
		}
	}

	immediate = {

		set_temp_variable = { loop_value = 0 }
		while_loop_effect = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_army_size = {
						size < 25
						type = armor
					}
					#check_variable = {
					#	loop_value < MAX_DIVISIONS_TO_SPAWN
					#}
				}
			}
			810 = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"German Medium Tank Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 1"
					owner = GER
					count = 1
				}
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					has_manpower > @ARMOR_DIVISION_MANPOWER
				}

					manpower_remove = @ARMOR_DIVISION_MANPOWER
				}
				multiply_temp_variable = {
					manpower_remove = -1
				}

				}
				set_temp_variable = {
					light_tank_aa_chassis_remove = @ARMOR_DIVISION_LIGHT_TANK_ANTI_AIR_EQUIPMENT
				}
				multiply_temp_variable = {
					light_tank_aa_chassis_remove = -1
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = light_tank_aa_chassis
					amount = light_tank_aa_chassis_remove
				}
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					has_equipment = {
						light_tank_chassis > @ARMOR_DIVISION_LIGHT_TANK_EQUIPMENT
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = {
					light_tank_equipment_remove = @ARMOR_DIVISION_LIGHT_TANK_EQUIPMENT
				}
				multiply_temp_variable = {
					light_tank_equipment_remove = -1
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = light_tank_chassis
					amount = light_tank_equipment_remove
				}
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					has_equipment = {
						medium_tank_chassis > @ARMOR_DIVISION_MEDIUM_TANK_EQUIPMENT
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = {
					medium_tank_equipment_remove = @ARMOR_DIVISION_MEDIUM_TANK_EQUIPMENT
				}
				multiply_temp_variable = {
					medium_tank_equipment_remove = -1
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = medium_tank_chassis
					amount = medium_tank_equipment_remove
				}
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					has_equipment = {
						medium_tank_infantry_support_chassis > @ARMOR_DIVISION_medium_tank_support_chassis
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = {
					medium_tank_infantry_support_chassis_remove = @ARMOR_DIVISION_medium_tank_support_chassis
				}
				multiply_temp_variable = {
					medium_tank_infantry_support_chassis_remove = -1
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = medium_tank_infantry_support_chassis
					amount = medium_tank_infantry_support_chassis_remove
				}
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = { loop_value = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = {}
